  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]

    if i % 2 == 0 {

    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  // By definition of DotProduct on sequences of equal length
  // we can unfold and use the induction on the length of `a'`.
  // The following `assert` shows that the invariant needed for the
  // lemma holds for the base case and the step.
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      // `DotProductAppend` gives us the needed relation between
      // DotProduct(a[..i+1], b + [a[i+1]]) and DotProduct(a[..i], b).
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      // After appending a[i+1], the dot product with the new prefix
      // of `a` should be unchanged (because a[i] * a[i+1] + a[i+1] * a[i]
      // cancels out).  We prove this explicitly.
      assert DotProduct(a[..i+1], b + [a[i + 1]]) == DotProduct(a[..i], b)
        + a[i] * a[i + 1] + a[i + 1] * a[i];
      assert DotProduct(a[..i+1], b + [a[i + 1]]) == DotProduct(a[..i], b);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      // After appending -a[i-1], the dot product with the new prefix
      // of `a` should be a[i-1] * a[i] (the expected value for odd
      // indices).  We prove this explicitly.
      assert DotProduct(a[..i+1], b + [-a[i - 1]]) == DotProduct(a[..i], b)
        + a[i] * (-a[i - 1]) + (-a[i - 1]) * a[i];
      assert DotProduct(a[..i+1], b + [-a[i - 1]]) == -a[i] * a[i - 1];
      assert DotProduct(a[..i+1], b + [-a[i - 1]]) == a[i - 1] * a[i];
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  var b' := b + [y];

  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  var b' := b + [y];

  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  // The following assertion replaces the previous one and is valid for all i
  // because the slice excludes the last element (the new element).
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
    decreases |a| - i
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a'[..|a'|-1], b'[..|b'|-1]) == DotProduct(a, b);
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
  assert DotProduct(a, b) == 0;
  assert AllNonZero(b);
  assert AllBounded(b, 100);
}

  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}
